<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Best little quick-stop fabric shop for fun, cheap finds--so many options in the $2-$6/yd range. Small selection but the inventory at this little locally owned store changes often so it's worth visiting frequently. Mostly synthetics, but always a few linen gems at great prices and always a selection of very affordable dupioni silk in a range of beautiful colors. Great stretch lace selection--fabric and trims, cheap zippers, notion, fasteners, and rhinestone trim of all kinds. Occasional leather scrap.<//Review>

I got Pad Thai with a spice level of 4 out of 10 and it's tolerable. My wife's green curry comes standard as a 3, and it's too hot for her... If you are kind of a wimp or novice when it comes to spice, I'd go with a 1 so you can taste and enjoy the wonderful flavor of the food. We also had the curry puffs and they were great! I chose to rate them a 3 instead of a 4 for the uncleanliness of the kitchen. It could be cleaned up a lot with a little effort. Other than that and the spice level, this place is great for a satisfying, and relatively inexpensive Thai dinner.

< Review>
The morning bun and banana cream tart are amazing. The bun is fluffy and flaky, which makes it a great texture as well as a nice baked food melting in your mouth. The banana cream tart isn't too sweet but has a nice texture to the banana cream. Super long line so go early if you want a seat and to beat the crowd. Another con is the prices for the baked goods but it is definitely worth the extra money.Bosco Bakery Cafe  the best bakery in CA.</Review>
